**Task & Context**  
Ops‑Monitor agent is managing a Blofin futures account. It must enforce portfolio rules, monitor health, and self‑heal any violations each trading cycle.

**Current Stack Health (2026‑07‑02 03:30:21 UTC)**  
- **Web‑socket cache age:** 1.2 s (fresh)  
- **Cycle:** 0 (first trading cycle)  
- **Account snapshot:** equity ≈ $3.05, available margin ≈ $0.94. Live API returned empty; system fell back to disk snapshot.  
- **Error:** HTTP 429 rate‑limit on `/api/v1/account/balance` (Cloudflare 1015). Flagged as `equity_error`.  
- **Universe:** 511 symbols (chromium_ws), cache age 78 s.  

**Portfolio**  
- **Open positions:** 1 short `VELVET‑USDT`  
  - Size: –1 contract  
  - Avg. entry: 1.5412, mark: 1.4584  
  - Unrealized PnL: +0.8279 (profitable)  
- **Blocked lists:**  
  - `blocked_inst_ids_for_new_buy`: []  
  - `blocked_inst_ids_for_new_sell`: ["VELVET‑USDT"] (cannot add to this short)  
- **Missing TP/SL:** ["VELVET‑USDT"] → violates rule “Every open position must have TP/SL”.  
- **Portfolio rules:**  
  1. No new buys on blocked‑buy list.  
  2. No new sells on blocked‑sell list.  
  3. If the only candidate is blocked, skip trade this cycle.  
  4. Must set TP/SL for all open positions (use `blofin_place_tpsl` or `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl`).  

**Learning / Self‑heal**  
- Last learning: “Swarm taught to self‑heal: User‑visible surfaces drifted from swarm logic”.  
- Last self‑fix: “Task audit failed cycle 1”. Indicates audit step failed, prompting repair.  

**Immediate Required Actions**  
1. **Protect open position:** Call `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl` (or `blofin_place_tpsl`) for `VELVET‑USDT` to set default TP (≈2.5 % above entry) and SL (≈1.5 % below entry).  
2. **Mitigate rate‑limit:** Implement back‑off/retry or rely on cached balance until API limit resets; avoid further 429 errors.  
3. **Re‑run task audit** after TP/SL is placed to clear the audit failure.  
4. **Trade decision:** Because the only open position is on a blocked‑sell instrument, the agent must either (a) skip adding more shorts this cycle, or (b) scan the universe (`blofin_rank_opportunities`) for an alternative short candidate not blocked.  

**Next Operational Step**  
- Execute `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl` for `VELVET‑USDT`.  
- Apply rate‑limit handling policy (back‑off, use cached balance).  
- Re‑audit tasks; if audit passes, proceed to next cycle or select a new trade per ranking.
